*   [go-resources (‚≠ê176)](https://github.com/omeid/go-resources) - Unfancy resources embedding with Go.
*   [go.rice (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/GeertJohan/go.rice) - go.rice is a Go package that makes working with resources such as HTML, JS, CSS, images, and templates very easy.
*   [mule (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/wlbr/mule) - Embed external resources like images, movies ... into Go source code to create single file binaries using `go generate`. Focussed on simplicity.
*   [packr (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/packr) - The simple and easy way to embed static files into Go binaries.
*   [rebed (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/soypat/rebed) - Recreate folder structures and files from Go 1.16's `embed.FS` type
*   [statics (‚≠ê66)](https://github.com/go-playground/statics) - Embeds static resources into go files for single binary compilation + works with http.FileSystem + symlinks.
*   [statik (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/rakyll/statik) - Embeds static files into a Go executable.
*   [templify (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/wlbr/templify) - Embed external template files into Go code to create single file binaries.
*   [vfsgen (‚≠ê964)](https://github.com/shurcooL/vfsgen) - Generates a vfsdata.go file that statically implements the given virtual filesystem.

### Science and Data Analysis

*   [assocentity (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/ndabAP/assocentity) - Package assocentity returns the average distance from words to a given entity.
*   [bradleyterry (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/seanhagen/bradleyterry) - Provides a Bradley-Terry Model for pairwise comparisons.
*   [calendarheatmap (‚≠ê368)](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/calendarheatmap) - Calendar heatmap in plain Go inspired by Github contribution activity.
*   [chart (‚≠ê750)](https://github.com/vdobler/chart) - Simple Chart Plotting library for Go. Supports many graphs types.
*   [dataframe-go (‚≠ê951)](https://github.com/rocketlaunchr/dataframe-go) - Dataframes for machine-learning and statistics (similar to pandas).
*   [decimal (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/db47h/decimal) - Package decimal implements arbitrary-precision decimal floating-point arithmetic.
*   [evaler (‚≠ê51)](https://github.com/soniah/evaler) - Simple floating point arithmetic expression evaluator.
*   [ewma (‚≠ê403)](https://github.com/VividCortex/ewma) - Exponentially-weighted moving averages.
*   [geom (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/skelterjohn/geom) - 2D geometry for golang.
*   [go-dsp (‚≠ê807)](https://github.com/mjibson/go-dsp) - Digital Signal Processing for Go.
*   [go-estimate (‚≠ê104)](https://github.com/milosgajdos/go-estimate) - State estimation and filtering algorithms in Go.
*   [go-gt (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/ThePaw/go-gt) - Graph theory algorithms written in "Go" language.
*   [godesim (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/soypat/godesim) - Extended/multivariable ODE solver framework for event-based simulations with simple API.
*   [goent (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/kzahedi/goent) - GO Implementation of Entropy Measures.
*   [gohistogram (‚≠ê170)](https://github.com/VividCortex/gohistogram) - Approximate histograms for data streams.
*   [gonum (‚≠ê6.4k)](https://github.com/gonum/gonum) - Gonum is a set of numeric libraries for the Go programming language. It contains libraries for matrices, statistics, optimization, and more.
*   [gonum/plot (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/gonum/plot) - gonum/plot provides an API for building and drawing plots in Go.
*   [goraph (‚≠ê709)](https://github.com/gyuho/goraph) - Pure Go graph theory library(data structure, algorithm visualization).
*   [gosl (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/cpmech/gosl) - Go scientific library for linear algebra, FFT, geometry, NURBS, numerical methods, probabilities, optimisation, differential equations, and more.
*   [GoStats (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/OGFris/GoStats) - GoStats is an Open Source GoLang library for math statistics mostly used in Machine Learning domains, it covers most of the Statistical measures functions.
*   [graph (‚≠ê630)](https://github.com/yourbasic/graph) - Library of basic graph algorithms.
*   [jsonl-graph (‚≠ê61)](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/jsonl-graph) - Tool to manipulate JSONL graphs with graphviz support.
*   [ode (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/ode) - Ordinary differential equation (ODE) solver which supports extended states and channel-based iteration stop conditions.
*   [orb (‚≠ê629)](https://github.com/paulmach/orb) - 2D geometry types with clipping, GeoJSON and Mapbox Vector Tile support.
*   [pagerank (‚≠ê79)](https://github.com/alixaxel/pagerank) - Weighted PageRank algorithm implemented in Go.
*   [piecewiselinear (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/sgreben/piecewiselinear) - Tiny linear interpolation library.
*   [PiHex (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/claygod/PiHex) - Implementation of the "Bailey-Borwein-Plouffe" algorithm for the hexadecimal number Pi.
*   [rootfinding (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/khezen/rootfinding) - root-finding algorithms library for finding roots of quadratic functions.
*   [sparse (‚≠ê137)](https://github.com/james-bowman/sparse) - Go Sparse matrix formats for linear algebra supporting scientific and machine learning applications, compatible with gonum matrix libraries.
*   [stats (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/montanaflynn/stats) - Statistics package with common functions missing from the Golang standard library.
*   [streamtools (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/nytlabs/streamtools) - general purpose, graphical tool for dealing with streams of data.
*   [TextRank (‚≠ê172)](https://github.com/DavidBelicza/TextRank) - TextRank implementation in Golang with extendable features (summarization, weighting, phrase extraction) and multithreading (goroutine) support.
*   [triangolatte (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/tchayen/triangolatte) - 2D triangulation library. Allows translating lines and polygons (both based on points) to the language of GPUs.

### Security

*   [acmetool (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.
*   [acra (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) - Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system.
*   [age (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability.
*   [argon2-hashing (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.
*   [argon2pw (‚≠ê89)](https://github.com/raja/argon2pw) - Argon2 password hash generation with constant-time password comparison.
*   [autocert](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/crypto/acme/autocert) - Auto provision Let's Encrypt certificates and start a TLS server.
*   [BadActor (‚≠ê312)](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.
*   [Cameradar (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/Ullaakut/cameradar) - Tool and library to remotely hack RTSP streams from surveillance cameras.
*   [certificates (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) - An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates.
*   [CertMagic (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) - Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal.
*   [dongle (‚≠ê673)](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding\&decoding and encryption\&decryption.
*   [firewalld-rest (‚≠ê331)](https://github.com/prashantgupta24/firewalld-rest) - A rest application to dynamically update firewalld rules on a linux server.
*   [go-generate-password (‚≠ê48)](https://github.com/m1/go-generate-password) - Password generator that can be used on the cli or as a library.
*   [go-htpasswd (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/tg123/go-htpasswd) - Apache htpasswd Parser for Go.
*   [go-password-validator (‚≠ê391)](https://github.com/lane-c-wagner/go-password-validator) - Password validator based on raw cryptographic entropy values.
*   [go-yara (‚≠ê286)](https://github.com/hillu/go-yara) - Go Bindings for [YARA (‚≠ê131)](https://github.com/plusvic/yara), the "pattern matching swiss knife for malware researchers (and everyone else)".
*   [goArgonPass (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/dwin/goArgonPass) - Argon2 password hash and verification designed to be compatible with existing Python and PHP implementations.
*   [goSecretBoxPassword (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/dwin/goSecretBoxPassword) - A probably paranoid package for securely hashing and encrypting passwords.
*   [Interpol](https://bitbucket.org/vahidi/interpol) - Rule-based data generator for fuzzing and penetration testing.
*   [lego (‚≠ê5.9k)](https://github.com/go-acme/lego) - Pure Go ACME client library and CLI tool (for use with Let's Encrypt).
*   [memguard (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/awnumar/memguard) - A pure Go library for handling sensitive values in memory.
*   [nacl (‚≠ê535)](https://github.com/kevinburke/nacl) - Go implementation of the NaCL set of API's.
*   [optimus-go (‚≠ê335)](https://github.com/pjebs/optimus-go) - ID hashing and Obfuscation using Knuth's Algorithm.
*   [passlib (‚≠ê282)](https://github.com/hlandau/passlib) - Futureproof password hashing library.
*   [secure (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/unrolled/secure) - HTTP middleware for Go that facilitates some quick security wins.
*   [secureio (‚≠ê29)](https://github.com/xaionaro-go/secureio) - An keyexchanging+authenticating+encrypting wrapper and multiplexer for `io.ReadWriteCloser` based on XChaCha20-poly1305, ECDH and ED25519.
*   [simple-scrypt (‚≠ê183)](https://github.com/elithrar/simple-scrypt) - Scrypt package with a simple, obvious API and automatic cost calibration built-in.
*   [ssh-vault (‚≠ê376)](https://github.com/ssh-vault/ssh-vault) - encrypt/decrypt using ssh keys.
*   [sslmgr (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/adrianosela/sslmgr) - SSL certificates made easy with a high level wrapper around acme/autocert.
*   [themis (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) - high-level cryptographic library for solving typical data security tasks (secure data storage, secure messaging, zero-knowledge proof authentication), available for 14 languages, best fit for multi-platform apps.

### Serialization

*   [asn1 (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/PromonLogicalis/asn1) - Asn.1 BER and DER encoding library for golang.
*   [bambam (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/glycerine/bambam) - generator for Cap'n Proto schemas from go.
*   [bel (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/32leaves/bel) - Generate TypeScript interfaces from Go structs/interfaces. Useful for JSON RPC.
*   [binstruct (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/ghostiam/binstruct) - Golang binary decoder for mapping data into the structure.
*   [cbor (‚≠ê535)](https://github.com/fxamacker/cbor) - Small, safe, and easy CBOR encoding and decoding library.
*   [colfer (‚≠ê689)](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/colfer) - Code generation for the Colfer binary format.
*   [csvutil (‚≠ê787)](https://github.com/jszwec/csvutil) - High Performance, idiomatic CSV record encoding and decoding to native Go structures.
*   [elastic (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/epiclabs-io/elastic) - Convert slices, maps or any other unknown value across different types at run-time, no matter what.
*   [fixedwidth (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/huydang284/fixedwidth) - Fixed-width text formatting (UTF-8 supported).
*   [fwencoder (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) - Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go.
*   [go-capnproto (‚≠ê287)](https://github.com/glycerine/go-capnproto) - Cap'n Proto library and parser for go.
*   [go-codec (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/ugorji/go) - High Performance, feature-Rich, idiomatic encode, decode and rpc library for msgpack, cbor and json, with runtime-based OR code-generation support.
*   [go-lctree (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/sbourlon/go-lctree) - Provides a CLI and primitives to serialize and deserialize [LeetCode binary trees](https://support.leetcode.com/hc/en-us/articles/360011883654-What-does-1-null-2-3-mean-in-binary-tree-representation).
*   [gogoprotobuf (‚≠ê5.5k)](https://github.com/gogo/protobuf) - Protocol Buffers for Go with Gadgets.
*   [goprotobuf (‚≠ê9k)](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) - Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers.
*   [jsoniter (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) - High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json".
*   [mapstructure (‚≠ê6.6k)](https://github.com/mitchellh/mapstructure) - Go library for decoding generic map values into native Go structures.
*   [php\_session\_decoder (‚≠ê157)](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) - GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions.
*   [pletter (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) - A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers.
*   [structomap (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) - Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures.
*   [unitpacking (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/recolude/unitpacking) - Library to pack unit vectors into as fewest bytes as possible.

### Server Applications

*   [algernon (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/xyproto/algernon) - HTTP/2 web server with built-in support for Lua, Markdown, GCSS and Amber.
*   [Caddy (‚≠ê46k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/caddy) - Caddy is an alternative, HTTP/2 web server that's easy to configure and use.
*   [consul](https://www.consul.io/) - Consul is a tool for service discovery, monitoring and configuration.
*   [cortex-tenant (‚≠ê63)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/cortex-tenant) - Prometheus remote write proxy that adds add Cortex tenant ID header based on metric labels.
*   [devd (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/cortesi/devd) - Local webserver for developers.
*   [discovery (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/Bilibili/discovery) - A registry for resilient mid-tier load balancing and failover.
*   [dudeldu (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/krotik/dudeldu) - A simple SHOUTcast server.
*   [dummy (‚≠ê169)](https://github.com/neotoolkit/dummy) - Run mock server based off an API contract with one command.
*   [Easegress (‚≠ê5.1k)](https://github.com/megaease/easegress) - A cloud native high availability/performance traffic orchestration system with observability and extensibility.
*   [etcd (‚≠ê43k)](https://github.com/coreos/etcd) - Highly-available key value store for shared configuration and service discovery.
*   [Euterpe (‚≠ê460)](https://github.com/ironsmile/euterpe) - Self-hosted music streaming server with built-in web UI and REST API.
*   [Fider (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/getfider/fider) - Fider is an open platform to collect and organize customer feedback.
*   [Flagr (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/checkr/flagr) - Flagr is an open-source feature flagging and A/B testing service.
*   [flipt (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/markphelps/flipt) - A self contained feature flag solution written in Go and Vue.js
*   [go-feature-flag (‚≠ê642)](https://github.com/thomaspoignant/go-feature-flag) - A feature flag solution, with only a YAML file in the backend (S3, GitHub, HTTP, local file ...), no server to install, just add a file in a central system and refer to it.
*   [go-proxy-cache (‚≠ê85)](https://github.com/fabiocicerchia/go-proxy-cache) - Simple Reverse Proxy with Caching, written in Go, using Redis.
*   [jackal (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/ortuman/jackal) - An XMPP server written in Go.
*   [lets-proxy2 (‚≠ê74)](https://github.com/rekby/lets-proxy2) - Reverse proxy for handle https with issue certificates in fly from lets-encrypt.
*   [minio (‚≠ê38k)](https://github.com/minio/minio) - Minio is a distributed object storage server.
*   [Moxy (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/moxy) - Moxy is a simple mocker and proxy application server, you can create mock endpoints as well as proxy requests in case no mock exists for the endpoint.
*   [nginx-prometheus (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/nginx-prometheus) - Nginx log parser and exporter to Prometheus.
*   [nsq](https://nsq.io/) - A realtime distributed messaging platform.
*   [protoxy (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/camgraff/protoxy) - A proxy server that converts JSON request bodies to Protocol Buffers.
*   [psql-streamer (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/psql-streamer) - Stream database events from PostgreSQL to Kafka.
*   [riemann-relay (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/riemann-relay) - Relay to load-balance Riemann events and/or convert them to Carbon.
*   [RoadRunner (‚≠ê7k)](https://github.com/spiral/roadrunner) - High-performance PHP application server, load-balancer and process manager.
*   [SFTPGo (‚≠ê5.7k)](https://github.com/drakkan/sftpgo) - Fully featured and highly configurable SFTP server with optional FTP/S and WebDAV support. It can serve local filesystem and Cloud Storage backends such as S3 and Google Cloud Storage.
*   [simple-jwt-provider (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/leberKleber/simple-jwt-provider) - Simple and lightweight provider which exhibits JWTs, supports login, password-reset (via mail) and user management.
*   [Trickster (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/tricksterproxy/trickster) - HTTP reverse proxy cache and time series accelerator.

### Stream Processing

*   [go-streams (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/reugn/go-streams) - Go stream processing library.
*   [machine (‚≠ê124)](https://github.com/whitaker-io/machine) - Go library for writing and generating stream workers with built in metrics and traceability.
*   [stream (‚≠ê75)](https://github.com/youthlin/stream) - Go Stream, like Java 8 Stream: Filter/Map/FlatMap/Peek/Sorted/ForEach/Reduce...

### Template Engines

*   [ego (‚≠ê547)](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) - Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled.
*   [extemplate (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/dannyvankooten/extemplate) - Tiny wrapper around html/template to allow for easy file-based template inheritance.
*   [fasttemplate (‚≠ê681)](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) - Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than [text/template](https://golang.org/pkg/text/template/).
*   [gospin (‚≠ê45)](https://github.com/m1/gospin) - Article spinning and spintax/spinning syntax engine, useful for A/B, testing pieces of text/articles and creating more natural conversations.
*   [goview (‚≠ê327)](https://github.com/foolin/goview) - Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application.
*   [jet (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/CloudyKit/jet) - Jet template engine.
*   [liquid (‚≠ê191)](https://github.com/osteele/liquid) - Go implementation of Shopify Liquid templates.
*   [maroto (‚≠ê947)](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) - A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple.
*   [pongo2 (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) - Django-like template-engine for Go.
*   [quicktemplate (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) - Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it.
*   [raymond (‚≠ê517)](https://github.com/aymerick/raymond) - Complete handlebars implementation in Go.
*   [Razor (‚≠ê809)](https://github.com/sipin/gorazor) - Razor view engine for Golang.
*   [Soy (‚≠ê168)](https://github.com/robfig/soy) - Closure templates (aka Soy templates) for Go, following the [official spec](https://developers.google.com/closure/templates/).
*   [sprig (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/Masterminds/sprig) - Useful template functions for Go templates.
*   [tbd (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/lucasepe/tbd) - A really simple way to create text templates with placeholders - exposes extra builtin Git repo metadata.

### Testing

*   Testing Frameworks

    *   [apitest](https://apitest.dev) - Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.
    *   [assert (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/go-playground/assert) - Basic Assertion Library used along side native go testing, with building blocks for custom assertions.
    *   [badio (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/cavaliercoder/badio) - Extensions to Go's `testing/iotest` package.
    *   [baloo (‚≠ê752)](https://github.com/h2non/baloo) - Expressive and versatile end-to-end HTTP API testing made easy.
    *   [be (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/be) - The minimalist generic test assertion library.
    *   [biff (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/fulldump/biff) - Bifurcation testing framework, BDD compatible.
    *   [charlatan (‚≠ê199)](https://github.com/percolate/charlatan) - Tool to generate fake interface implementations for tests.
    *   [commander (‚≠ê212)](https://github.com/SimonBaeumer/commander) - Tool for testing cli applications on windows, linux and osx.
    *   [covergates (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/covergates/covergates) - Self-hosted code coverage report review and management service.
    *   [cupaloy (‚≠ê255)](https://github.com/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy) - Simple snapshot testing addon for your test framework.
    *   [dbcleaner (‚≠ê150)](https://github.com/khaiql/dbcleaner) - Clean database for testing purpose, inspired by `database_cleaner` in Ruby.
    *   [dsunit (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/viant/dsunit) - Datastore testing for SQL, NoSQL, structured files.
    *   [embedded-postgres (‚≠ê549)](https://github.com/fergusstrange/embedded-postgres) - Run a real Postgres database locally on Linux, OSX or Windows as part of another Go application or test.
    *   [endly (‚≠ê236)](https://github.com/viant/endly) - Declarative end to end functional testing.
    *   [fixenv (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/rekby/fixenv) - Fixture manage engine, inspired by pytest fixtures.
    *   [flute (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/suzuki-shunsuke/flute) - HTTP client testing framework.
    *   [frisby (‚≠ê273)](https://github.com/verdverm/frisby) - REST API testing framework.
    *   [gherkingen (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/hedhyw/gherkingen) - BDD boilerplate generator and framework.
    *   [ginkgo](https://onsi.github.io/ginkgo/) - BDD Testing Framework for Go.
    *   [gnomock (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/orlangure/gnomock) - integration testing with real dependencies (database, cache, even Kubernetes or AWS) running in Docker, without mocks.
    *   [go-carpet (‚≠ê236)](https://github.com/msoap/go-carpet) - Tool for viewing test coverage in terminal.
    *   [go-cmp (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/google/go-cmp) - Package for comparing Go values in tests.
    *   [go-hit (‚≠ê187)](https://github.com/Eun/go-hit) - Hit is an http integration test framework written in golang.
    *   [go-mutesting (‚≠ê577)](https://github.com/zimmski/go-mutesting) - Mutation testing for Go source code.
    *   [go-mysql-test-container (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/arikama/go-mysql-test-container) - Golang MySQL testcontainer to help with MySQL integration testing.
    *   [go-snaps (‚≠ê54)](http://github.com/gkampitakis/go-snaps) - Jest-like snapshot testing in Golang.
    *   [go-testdeep (‚≠ê343)](https://github.com/maxatome/go-testdeep) - Extremely flexible golang deep comparison, extends the go testing package.
    *   [go-testpredicate (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/maargenton/go-testpredicate) - Test predicate style assertions library with extensive diagnostics output.
    *   [go-vcr (‚≠ê987)](https://github.com/dnaeon/go-vcr) - Record and replay your HTTP interactions for fast, deterministic and accurate tests.
    *   [goblin (‚≠ê881)](https://github.com/franela/goblin) - Mocha like testing framework fo Go.
    *   [goc (‚≠ê637)](https://github.com/qiniu/goc) - Goc is a comprehensive coverage testing system for The Go Programming Language.
    *   [gocheck](https://labix.org/gocheck) - More advanced testing framework alternative to gotest.
    *   [GoConvey (‚≠ê7.6k)](https://github.com/smartystreets/goconvey/) - BDD-style framework with web UI and live reload.
    *   [gocrest (‚≠ê86)](https://github.com/corbym/gocrest) - Composable hamcrest-like matchers for Go assertions.
    *   [godog (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/cucumber/godog) - Cucumber BDD framework for Go.
    *   [gofight (‚≠ê433)](https://github.com/appleboy/gofight) - API Handler Testing for Golang Router framework.
    *   [gogiven (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/corbym/gogiven) - YATSPEC-like BDD testing framework for Go.
    *   [gomatch (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/jfilipczyk/gomatch) - library created for testing JSON against patterns.
    *   [gomega](https://onsi.github.io/gomega/) - Rspec like matcher/assertion library.
    *   [Gont (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/stv0g/gont) - Go network testing toolkit for testing building complex network topologies using Linux namespaces.
    *   [GoSpec (‚≠ê113)](https://github.com/orfjackal/gospec) - BDD-style testing framework for the Go programming language.
    *   [gospecify (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/stesla/gospecify) - This provides a BDD syntax for testing your Go code. It should be familiar to anybody who has used libraries such as rspec.
    *   [gosuite (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/pavlo/gosuite) - Brings lightweight test suites with setup/teardown facilities to `testing` by leveraging Go1.7's Subtests.
    *   [got (‚≠ê261)](https://github.com/ysmood/got) - An enjoyable golang test framework.
    *   [gotest.tools (‚≠ê404)](https://github.com/gotestyourself/gotest.tools) - A collection of packages to augment the go testing package and support common patterns.
    *   [Hamcrest (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/rdrdr/hamcrest) - fluent framework for declarative Matcher objects that, when applied to input values, produce self-describing results.
    *   [httpexpect (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/gavv/httpexpect) - Concise, declarative, and easy to use end-to-end HTTP and REST API testing.
    *   [is (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/matryer/is) - Professional lightweight testing mini-framework for Go.
    *   [jsonassert (‚≠ê103)](https://github.com/kinbiko/jsonassert) - Package for verifying that your JSON payloads are serialized correctly.
    *   [omg.testingtools (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.testingtools) - The simple library for change a values of private fields for testing.
    *   [restit (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/yookoala/restit) - Go micro framework to help writing RESTful API integration test.
    *   [schema (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/jgroeneveld/schema) - Quick and easy expression matching for JSON schemas used in requests and responses.
    *   [stop-and-go (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/elgohr/stop-and-go) - Testing helper for concurrency.
    *   [testcase (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/adamluzsi/testcase) - Idiomatic testing framework for Behavior Driven Development.
    *   [testcontainers-go (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/testcontainers/testcontainers-go) - A Go package that makes it simple to create and clean up container-based dependencies for automated integration/smoke tests. The clean, easy-to-use API enables developers to programmatically define containers that should be run as part of a test and clean up those resources when the test is done.
    *   [testfixtures (‚≠ê912)](https://github.com/go-testfixtures/testfixtures) - A helper for Rails' like test fixtures to test database applications.
    *   [Testify (‚≠ê19k)](https://github.com/stretchr/testify) - Sacred extension to the standard go testing package.
    *   [testmd](https://godoc.org/github.com/tvastar/test/cmd/testmd) - Convert markdown snippets into testable go code.
    *   [testsql (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/zhulongcheng/testsql) - Generate test data from SQL files before testing and clear it after finished.
    *   [testza (‚≠ê408)](https://github.com/MarvinJWendt/testza) - Full-featured test framework with nice colorized output.
    *   [trial (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/jgroeneveld/trial) - Quick and easy extendable assertions without introducing much boilerplate.
    *   [Tt (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/vcaesar/tt) - Simple and colorful test tools.
    *   [wstest (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/posener/wstest) - Websocket client for unit-testing a websocket http.Handler.
*   Mock

    *   [counterfeiter (‚≠ê789)](https://github.com/maxbrunsfeld/counterfeiter) - Tool for generating self-contained mock objects.
    *   [genmock](https://gitlab.com/so_literate/genmock) - Go mocking system with code generator for building calls of the interface methods.
    *   [go-localstack (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/elgohr/go-localstack) - Tool for using localstack in AWS testing.
    *   [go-sqlmock (‚≠ê5.1k)](https://github.com/DATA-DOG/go-sqlmock) - Mock SQL driver for testing database interactions.
    *   [go-txdb (‚≠ê517)](https://github.com/DATA-DOG/go-txdb) - Single transaction based database driver mainly for testing purposes.
    *   [gock (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/h2non/gock) - Versatile HTTP mocking made easy.
    *   [gomock (‚≠ê8.6k)](https://github.com/golang/mock) - Mocking framework for the Go programming language.
    *   [govcr (‚≠ê141)](https://github.com/seborama/govcr) - HTTP mock for Golang: record and replay HTTP interactions for offline testing.
    *   [hoverfly (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/SpectoLabs/hoverfly) - HTTP(S) proxy for recording and simulating REST/SOAP APIs with extensible middleware and easy-to-use CLI.
    *   [httpmock (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/jarcoal/httpmock) - Easy mocking of HTTP responses from external resources.
    *   [minimock (‚≠ê485)](https://github.com/gojuno/minimock) - Mock generator for Go interfaces.
    *   [mockery (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/vektra/mockery) - Tool to generate Go interfaces.
    *   [mockhttp (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/tv42/mockhttp) - Mock object for Go http.ResponseWriter.
    *   [mockit (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/pasdam/mockit) - Allows functions and method easy mocking, without defining new types; it's similar to Mockito for Java.
    *   [mooncake (‚≠ê17)](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/mooncake) - A simple way to generate mocks for multiple purposes
    *   [timex (‚≠ê66)](https://github.com/cabify/timex) - A test-friendly replacement for the native `time` package.
*   Fuzzing and delta-debugging/reducing/shrinking.

    *   [go-fuzz (‚≠ê4.6k)](https://github.com/dvyukov/go-fuzz) - Randomized testing system.
    *   [gofuzz (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/google/gofuzz) - Library for populating go objects with random values.
    *   [Tavor (‚≠ê242)](https://github.com/zimmski/tavor) - Generic fuzzing and delta-debugging framework.
*   Selenium and browser control tools.

    *   [cdp (‚≠ê666)](https://github.com/mafredri/cdp) - Type-safe bindings for the Chrome Debugging Protocol that can be used with browsers or other debug targets that implement it.
    *   [chromedp (‚≠ê8.7k)](https://github.com/knq/chromedp) - a way to drive/test Chrome, Safari, Edge, Android Webviews, and other browsers supporting the Chrome Debugging Protocol.
    *   [ggr (‚≠ê301)](https://github.com/aerokube/ggr) - a lightweight server that routes and proxies Selenium WebDriver requests to multiple Selenium hubs.
    *   [playwright-go (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/mxschmitt/playwright-go) - browser automation library to control Chromium, Firefox and WebKit with a single API.
    *   [rod (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/go-rod/rod) - A Devtools driver to make web automation and scraping easy.
    *   [selenoid (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/aerokube/selenoid) - alternative Selenium hub server that launches browsers within containers.
*   Fail injection
    *   [failpoint (‚≠ê766)](https://github.com/pingcap/failpoint) - An implementation of [failpoints](https://www.freebsd.org/cgi/man.cgi?query=fail) for Golang.

*   [go-lark (‚≠ê137)](https://github.com/go-lark/lark) - An easy-to-use unofficial SDK for [Feishu](https://open.feishu.cn/) and [Lark](https://open.larksuite.com/) Open Platform.

*   [go-sophos (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/esurdam/go-sophos) - Go client library for the [Sophos UTM REST API](https://www.sophos.com/en-us/medialibrary/PDFs/documentation/UTMonAWS/Sophos-UTM-RESTful-API.pdf?la=en) with zero dependencies.

*   [scany (‚≠ê865)](https://github.com/georgysavva/scany) - Library for scanning data from a database into Go structs and more.
*   [serve (‚≠ê289)](https://github.com/syntaqx/serve) - A static http server anywhere you need.
*   [set (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/nofeaturesonlybugs/set) - Performant and flexible struct mapping and loose type conversion.
*   [shutdown (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/ztrue/shutdown) - App shutdown hooks for `os.Signal` handling.
*   [silk (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/chrispassas/silk) - Read silk netflow files.
*   [slice (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/psampaz/slice) - Type-safe functions for common Go slice operations.
*   [sliceconv (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/Henry-Sarabia/sliceconv) - Slice conversion between primitive types.
*   [slicer (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/leaanthony/slicer) - Makes working with slices easier.
*   [sorty (‚≠ê117)](https://github.com/jfcg/sorty) - Fast Concurrent / Parallel Sorting.
*   [sqlx (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/jmoiron/sqlx) - provides a set of extensions on top of the excellent built-in database/sql package.
*   [sshman (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/shoobyban/sshman) - SSH Manager for authorized\_keys files on multiple remote servers.
*   [statiks (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/janiltonmaciel/statiks) - Fast, zero-configuration, static HTTP filer server.
*   [Storm (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/asdine/storm) - Simple and powerful toolkit for BoltDB.
*   [structs (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/PumpkinSeed/structs) - Implement simple functions to manipulate structs.
*   [throttle (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/yudppp/throttle) - Throttle is an object that will perform exactly one action per duration.
*   [tik (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/andy2046/tik) - Simple and easy timing wheel package for Go.
*   [tome (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/cyruzin/tome) - Tome was designed to paginate simple RESTful APIs.
*   [toolbox (‚≠ê186)](https://github.com/viant/toolbox) - Slice, map, multimap, struct, function, data conversion utilities. Service router, macro evaluator, tokenizer.
*   [ugo (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/alxrm/ugo) - ugo is slice toolbox with concise syntax for Go.
*   [UNIS (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/esemplastic/unis) - Common Architecture‚Ñ¢ for String Utilities in Go.
*   [usql (‚≠ê7.9k)](https://github.com/knq/usql) - usql is a universal command-line interface for SQL databases.
*   [util (‚≠ê272)](https://github.com/shomali11/util) - Collection of useful utility functions. (strings, concurrency, manipulations, ...).
*   [wuzz (‚≠ê10k)](https://github.com/asciimoo/wuzz) - Interactive cli tool for HTTP inspection.
*   [xferspdy (‚≠ê96)](https://github.com/monmohan/xferspdy) - Xferspdy provides binary diff and patch library in golang.

### UUID

*   [goid (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) - Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs.
*   [gouid (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) - Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation.
*   [nanoid (‚≠ê58)](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) - A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator.
*   [sno (‚≠ê79)](https://github.com/muyo/sno) - Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata.
*   [ulid (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) - Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier).
*   [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq) - No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/agext/uuid) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) - Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê4.2k)](https://github.com/google/uuid) - Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services.
*   [wuid (‚≠ê485)](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) - An extremely fast globally unique number generator.
*   [xid (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/rs/xid) - Xid is a globally unique id generator library, ready to be safely used directly in your server code.

### Validation

*   [checkdigit (‚≠ê97)](https://github.com/osamingo/checkdigit) - Provide check digit algorithms (Luhn, Verhoeff, Damm) and calculators (ISBN, EAN, JAN, UPC, etc.).
*   [gody (‚≠ê63)](https://github.com/guiferpa/gody) - :balloon: A lightweight struct validator for Go.
*   [govalid (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/twharmon/govalid) - Fast, tag-based validation for structs.
*   [govalidator (‚≠ê5.6k)](https://github.com/asaskevich/govalidator) - Validators and sanitizers for strings, numerics, slices and structs.
*   [govalidator (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/govalidator) - Validate Golang request data with simple rules. Highly inspired by Laravel's request validation.
*   [jio (‚≠ê72)](https://github.com/faceair/jio) - jio is a json schema validator similar to [joi (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/hapijs/joi).
*   [ozzo-validation (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-validation) - Supports validation of various data types (structs, strings, maps, slices, etc.) with configurable and extensible validation rules specified in usual code constructs instead of struct tags.
*   [validate (‚≠ê854)](https://github.com/gookit/validate) - Go package for data validation and filtering. support validate Map, Struct, Request(Form, JSON, url.Values, Uploaded Files) data and more features.
*   [validate (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/validate) - This package provides a framework for writing validations for Go applications.
*   [validator (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/go-playground/validator) - Go Struct and Field validation, including Cross Field, Cross Struct, Map, Slice and Array diving.

### Middlewares / Actual middlewares

*   [client-timing (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
*   [CORS (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/rs/cors) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
*   [formjson (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/rs/formjson) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
*   [go-fault (‚≠ê475)](https://github.com/github/go-fault) - Fault injection middleware for Go.
*   [go-server-timing (‚≠ê851)](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) - Add/parse Server-Timing header.
*   [Limiter (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
*   [ln-paywall (‚≠ê132)](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
*   [mid (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/bobg/mid) - Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more.
*   [rk-gin (‚≠ê40)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [rk-grpc (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [Tollbooth (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
*   [XFF (‚≠ê96)](https://github.com/sebest/xff) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

### Middlewares / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alice (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/justinas/alice) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
*   [catena (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
*   [chain (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
*   [go-wrap](https://github.com/go-on/wrap) - Small middlewares package for net/http.
*   [gores (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
*   [interpose (‚≠ê297)](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
*   [mediary (‚≠ê82)](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) - add interceptors to `http.Client` to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
*   [muxchain (‚≠ê209)](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
*   [negroni (‚≠ê7.3k)](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
*   [render (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/unrolled/render) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
*   [renderer (‚≠ê253)](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) - Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go.
*   [rye (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.
*   [stats (‚≠ê588)](https://github.com/thoas/stats) - Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.

### Routers / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alien (‚≠ê126)](https://github.com/gernest/alien) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
*   [bellt (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt) - A simple Go HTTP router.
*   [Bone (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) - Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
*   [Bxog (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) - Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
*   [chi (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) - Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
*   [fasthttprouter (‚≠ê874)](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) - High performance router forked from `httprouter`. The first router fit for `fasthttp`.
*   [FastRouter (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/razonyang/fastrouter) - a fast, flexible HTTP router written in Go.
*   [gocraft/web (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/gocraft/web) - Mux and middleware package in Go.
*   [Goji (‚≠ê935)](https://github.com/goji/goji) - Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for `net/context`.
*   [goroute (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/goroute/route) - Simple yet powerful HTTP request multiplexer.
*   [GoRouter (‚≠ê146)](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) - GoRouter is a Server/API micro framework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting `net/context`.
*   [gowww/router (‚≠ê164)](https://github.com/gowww/router) - Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
*   [httprouter (‚≠ê15k)](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
*   [httptreemux (‚≠ê581)](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
*   [lars (‚≠ê387)](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
*   [mux (‚≠ê18k)](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
*   [ngamux (‚≠ê58)](https://github.com/ngamux/ngamux) - Simple HTTP router for Go.
*   [ozzo-routing (‚≠ê448)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
*   [pure (‚≠ê134)](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
*   [Siesta (‚≠ê352)](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) - Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
*   [vestigo (‚≠ê268)](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) - Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
*   [violetear (‚≠ê106)](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) - Go HTTP router.
*   [xmux (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/rs/xmux) - High performance muxer based on `httprouter` with `net/context` support.
*   [xujiajun/gorouter (‚≠ê533)](https://github.com/xujiajun/gorouter) - A simple and fast HTTP router for Go.

### XML / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

### Zero Trust / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [Cosign (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/sigstore/cosign) - Container Signing, Verification and Storage in an OCI registry.
*   [in-toto (‚≠ê77)](https://github.com/in-toto/in-toto-golang) - Go implementation of the in-toto (provides a framework to protect the integrity of the software supply chain) python reference implementation.
*   [Spiffe-Vault (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/philips-labs/spiffe-vault) - Utilizes Spiffe JWT authentication with Hashicorp Vault for secretless authentication.
*   [Spire (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/spiffe/spire) - SPIRE (the SPIFFE Runtime Environment) is a toolchain of APIs for establishing trust between software systems across a wide variety of hosting platforms.

*   [ide (‚≠ê354)](https://github.com/thestrukture/ide) - Browser accessible IDE. Designed for Go with Go.
*   [ipe (‚≠ê363)](https://github.com/dimiro1/ipe) - Open source Pusher server implementation compatible with Pusher client libraries written in GO.
*   [joincap (‚≠ê182)](https://github.com/assafmo/joincap) - Command-line utility for merging multiple pcap files together.
*   [Juju](https://jujucharms.com/) - Cloud-agnostic service deployment and orchestration - supports EC2, Azure, Openstack, MAAS and more.
*   [Leaps (‚≠ê732)](https://github.com/jeffail/leaps) - Pair programming service using Operational Transforms.
*   [lgo (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/yunabe/lgo) - Interactive Go programming with Jupyter. It supports code completion, code inspection and 100% Go compatibility.
*   [limetext](https://limetext.github.io) - Lime Text is a powerful and elegant text editor primarily developed in Go that aims to be a Free and open-source software successor to Sublime Text.
*   [LiteIDE (‚≠ê7.2k)](https://github.com/visualfc/liteide) - LiteIDE is a simple, open source, cross-platform Go IDE.
*   [mockingjay (‚≠ê533)](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) - Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests.
*   [myLG (‚≠ê2.6k)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) - Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go.
*   [naclpipe (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) - Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go.
*   [Neo-cowsay (‚≠ê243)](https://github.com/Code-Hex/Neo-cowsay) - üêÆ cowsay is reborn. for a New Era.
*   [nes (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) emulator written in Go.
*   [Orbit (‚≠ê175)](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) - A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates.
*   [peg (‚≠ê898)](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) - Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator.
*   [Plik (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/root-gg/plik) - Plik is a temporary file upload system (Wetransfer like) in Go.
*   [protoncheck (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/servusdei2018/protoncheck) - ProtonMail module for waybar/polybar/yabar/i3blocks.
*   [restic (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/restic/restic) - De-duplicating backup program.
*   [scc (‚≠ê4.5k)](https://github.com/boyter/scc) - Sloc Cloc and Code, a very fast accurate code counter with complexity calculations and COCOMO estimates.
*   [Seaweed File System (‚≠ê17k)](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) disk seek.
*   [shell2http (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control).
*   [snap (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/intelsdi-x/snap) - Powerful telemetry framework.
*   [Snitch (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/lucasgomide/snitch) - Simple way to notify your team and many tools when someone has deployed any application via Tsuru.
*   [Stack Up (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/pressly/sup) - Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers.
*   [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/) - Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
*   [tcpdog (‚≠ê217)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpdog) - eBPF based TCP observability.
*   [tcpprobe (‚≠ê334)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpprobe) - TCP tool for network performance and path monitoring, including socket statistics.
*   [term-quiz (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/crazcalm/term-quiz) - Quizzes for your terminal.
*   [toxiproxy (‚≠ê8.9k)](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) - Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests.
*   [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/) - Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
*   [vaku (‚≠ê146)](https://github.com/lingrino/vaku) - CLI & API for folder-based functions in Vault like copy, move, and search.
*   [vFlow (‚≠ê961)](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) - High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector.
*   [wellington (‚≠ê302)](https://github.com/wellington/wellington) - Sass project management tool, extends the language with sprite functions (like Compass).
*   [woke (‚≠ê368)](https://github.com/get-woke/woke) - Detect non-inclusive language in your source code.

*   [gospeed (‚≠ê111)](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
*   [kvbench (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark.

## [13. Awesome Snmp](/content/eozer/awesome-snmp/week/README.md)

### Libraries / C/C++

*   [net-snmp](http://www.net-snmp.org/) - A suite of software for using and deploying the SNMP protocol (v1, v2c and v3 and the AgentX subagent protocol). Contains also Python bindings.
*   [SNMP++](https://www.agentpp.com/api/cpp/snmp_pp.html) - BSD licensed SNMP implemention from HP. Supports SNMP v1/2c/v3, thread-safety, and many more.
*   [AGENT++](https://www.agentpp.com/api/cpp/agent_pp.html) - The AGENT++ C++ framework provides a complete tri-lingual SNMP v1/2c/3 protocol engine and dispatcher for the development of SNMP agents. Apache licensed.
*   [AgentX++](https://www.agentpp.com/api/cpp/agentx_pp.html) - The AgentX++ C++ framework provides a complete AgentX protocol (RFC 2741) implementation that adds AgentX master and sub-agent support to AGENT++ (`Commercial`).
*   [openSNMP](https://sourceforge.net/projects/opensnmp/) - BSD licensed multi-threaded implementation of SNMPv3.

### Libraries / C#

*   [sharpSNMP (‚≠ê303)](https://github.com/lextudio/sharpsnmplib) - MIT licensed SNMP library for .NET/Xamarin/Mono.
*   [SnmpSharpNet (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/rqx110/SnmpSharpNet) - Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP) .Net library written in C# (csharp). Implements protocol version 1, 2 and 3.

### Libraries / Go

*   [gosnmp/gosnmp (‚≠ê933)](https://github.com/gosnmp/gosnmp) - An SNMP library written in Go. It provides Get, GetNext, GetBulk, Walk, BulkWalk, Set and Traps. It supports IPv4/IPv6, using SNMP v1/v2c/v3.

### Libraries / Java

*   [SNMP4J](https://www.agentpp.com/api/java/snmp4j.html) - SNMP4J is an enterprise class, free open source, and state-of-the-art SNMP v1/2c/v3 implementation for Java‚Ñ¢.
*   [SNMP4J-Agent](https://www.agentpp.com/api/java/snmp4jagent.html) - SNMP4J-Agent is a Java‚Ñ¢ API on top of the core SNMP4J API for the development of SNMP agents (command responders).
*   [joeSNMP](https://sourceforge.net/projects/joesnmp/) - joeSNMP is an open-source Java SNMP class library published under the LGPL.
*   [Westhawk's SNMP](https://snmp.westhawk.co.uk/) - An open-sourced Java library that can be used for SNMP v1/v2c/v3. Supports traps, authentication and privacy. As authentication protocols it offers MD5 and SHA1.
*   [mibble (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/cederberg/mibble) - Mibble is an open-source SNMP MIB (or SMI) parser library for Java.

### Libraries / JavaScript

*   [node-net-snmp (‚≠ê166)](https://github.com/markabrahams/node-net-snmp) -  JavaScript implementation of the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP), implements versions 1, 2c and 3.
*   [node-snmp-native (‚≠ê247)](https://github.com/calmh/node-snmp-native) -  Native JavaScript SNMP library for Node.js.
*   [node-snmpjs (‚≠ê111)](https://github.com/joyent/node-snmpjs) - This package provides a toolkit for SNMP agents and management applications in Node.js.
*   [snmp-node (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/neias/snmp-node) - Native JavaScript SNMP library for Node.js.

### Tools / CLIs

*   [SNMP4JCLT](https://www.agentpp.com/tools/snmp4jclt.html) - Use the SNMP4J Command Line Tool (CLT) to send SNMPv1/v2c/v3 requests and traps to a target with IPv4 or v6 based UDP, TCP, or TLSv1,2 transport (`Commercial`).

### Tools / GUIs

*   [tkmib](http://www.net-snmp.org/) - A perl/Tk interactive graphical MIB browser for SNMP.
*   [agentpp/MIB Designer](https://www.agentpp.com/tools/mibdesigner.html) - Use MIB Designer to create, edit, manage, and explore SMI specifications (`Commercial`).
*   [agentpp/MIB Explorer Pro](https://www.agentpp.com/tools/mibexplorer.html) - Use MIB Explorer to browse, configure, test\&debug, monitor, and discover SNMPv1/2c/3 entities.
*   [sharpsnmp/SNMP Pro](https://www.sharpsnmp.com/) - A family of .NET based SNMP products, including the commercial MIB Compiler, MIB Assembly, and the open source Library.

### Publications / RFCs

*   [rfc1098](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc1098.txt) - A Simple Network Management Protocol (version 1).
*   [rfc1155](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc1155.txt) - Structure and Identification of Management Information.
*   [rfc2578](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2578.txt) - Structure of Management Information Version 2 (SMIv2).
*   [rfc2741](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2741.txt) - Agent Extensibility (AgentX) Protocol Version 1.
*   [rfc2742](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2742.txt) - Definitions of Managed Objects for Extensible SNMP Agents.
*   [rfc3410](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3410.txt) - Introduction and Applicability Statements for Internet Standard Management Framework.
*   [rfc3411](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3411.txt) - An Architecture for Describing Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP) Management Frameworks.
*   [rfc3412](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3412.txt) - Message Processing and Dispatching for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc3413](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3413.txt) - Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP) Applications.
*   [rfc3414](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3414.txt) - User-based Security Model (USM) for version 3 of the
    Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMPv3).
*   [rfc3415](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3415.txt) - View-based Access Control Model (VACM) for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc3416](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3416.txt) - Version 2 of the Protocol Operations for the Simple
    Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc3417](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3417.txt) - Transport Mappings for the Simple Network Management
    Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc3418](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3418.txt) - Management Information Base (MIB) for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc3584](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3584.txt) - Coexistence between Version 1, Version 2, and Version 3 of the Internet-standard Network Management Framework.
*   [rfc3826](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3826.txt) - The Advanced Encryption Standard (AES) Cipher Algorithm
    in the SNMP User-based Security Model.
*   [rfc4088](https://tools.ietf.org/rfc/rfc4088.txt) - Uniform Resource Identifier (URI) Scheme for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc5343](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5343.txt) - Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP) Context EngineID Discovery.
*   [rfc5590](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5590.txt) - Transport Subsystem for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc5591](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5591.txt) - Transport Subsystem for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc5592](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5592.txt) - Secure Shell Transport Model for the Simple Network Management Protocol (SNMP).
*   [rfc7630](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7630.txt) - HMAC-SHA-2 Authentication Protocols in the User-based Security Model (USM) for SNMPv3.

## [18. Awesome Open Source Games](/content/michelpereira/awesome-open-source-games/week/README.md)

### Browser-Based / Boardgame

*   [Desperate Gods (‚≠ê305)](https://github.com/David20321/FTJ) - Free online board game that was designed to be played just like a board game in real-life: no rules are enforced by the computer.
*   [Green Mahjong (‚≠ê77)](https://github.com/danbeck/green-mahjong) - Solitaire mahjong game done in HTML/CSS/JavaScript.

### Browser-Based / Arcade

*   [Captain Rogers (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/EnclaveGames/Captain-Rogers) - Captain Rogers: Asteroid Belt of Sirius - HTML5 mobile game created using ImpactJavaScript.
*   [CHANG‚Ç¨ (‚≠ê43)](https://github.com/RothschildGames/change) - Intense game about the extreme life of supermarket cashiers.
*   [Clumsy Bird (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/ellisonleao/clumsy-bird) - Flappy Bird clone in JavaScript using MelonJavaScript.
*   [Coffee Snake (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/dommmel/coffee-snake) - HTML5 snake game written in CoffeeScript.
*   [Coil (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/leereilly/Coil) - HTML5 canvas game where you defeat enemies by wrapping enemies in your trail.
*   [Color Quest (‚≠ê37)](https://github.com/redbluegames/game-off-2013) - Infinite runner following a black and white pixel's quest to change into a color pixel.
*   [Custom Tetris (‚≠ê86)](https://github.com/ondras/custom-tetris) - Play the classic Tetris game the way you like it.
*   [D3shooter (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/nsmirn0v/d3shooter) - Asteroids style game in HTML5 as a demo of the d3 library.
*   [DuckHunt JavaScript](https://github.com/MattSurabian/DuckHunt-JavaScript) - DuckHunt ported to JavaScript and HTML5 with a level creator.
*   [Fluid Table Tennis (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/anirudhjoshi/fluid_table_tennis) - Renders a table tennis game interacting with a full-color real-time fluid simulation at 60 FPS.
*   [HotFix (‚≠ê202)](https://github.com/sdrdis/hotfix) - Help Hotfix collect stargazers and avoid enemies. Collect commits to upgrade hotfix and add new features.
*   [I Spy A Ghost (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/OmarShehata/I-Spy-A-Ghost) - An experimental p2p multiplayer game made in HTML5/Phaser using WebRTC.
*   [Pappu Pakia (‚≠ê435)](https://github.com/mindd-it/pappu-pakia) - Addictive game where you guide little Pappu around obstacles while collecting coins, stars, and berries and avoiding enemies known as Pakias.
*   [Snake\_new (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/RabiRoshan/snake_game) - Classic nokia snake game using web.
*   [Spashal (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/MrRar/spashal) - Danger lurks around every corner in space.
*   [Square Off! (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/ScriptaGames/SquareOff) - Multiplayer 1v1 air-hockey style game, place squares to deflect the ball.
*   [Space Crusade (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/Loopeex/space-crusade) - HTML5 game developped with PhaserJavaScript Framework.
*   [Super Mario Bros (‚≠ê166)](https://github.com/martindrapeau/backbone-game-engine) - Super Mario Bros level one written with Backbone Game Engine.
*   [Survivor (‚≠ê116)](https://github.com/scottschiller/SURVIVOR) - Playable HTML + CSS + JavaScript remake of a space-based "shoot-'em-up" arcade game for Atari / Commodore 64 from 1982, including a level editor and design tool.

### Browser-Based / FPS

*   [BananaBread (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/kripken/BananaBread) - Port of the Cube 2/Sauerbraten 3D game engine/first person shooter to the web, compiling C++ and OpenGL to JavaScript and WebGL using Emscripten.

### Browser-Based / MMORPG

### Browser-Based / Puzzle

*   [Beatrix (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/cxong/Beatrix) - Music game where you arrange the drums to catch the beats and play the right rhythm.
*   [BitBot (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/recardona/BitBot) - HTML/JavaScript game where you control a bot, which must sense, plan, and act.
*   [BlicblockJavaScript (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/cheshire137/blicblock-js) - JavaScript game based on Blicblock in The Sims 4. Match tetrominoes to clear the board.
*   [Blockrain.js (‚≠ê915)](https://github.com/Aerolab/blockrain.js) - Embed & play the classic game on your site. Simple as that.
*   [Branching Out (‚≠ê66)](https://github.com/thehen/game-off-2012) - Minimalist game about leaving home.

*   [Push and Fork (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/Octocarina/game-off-2012) - Puzzle game in which you carry a fork, push blocks, and go back in time.
*   [Shape Experiment (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/binarymax/shape) - The shape recognition reflex game.
*   [Sudoku JavaScript (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/baruchel/sudoku-js) - A Sudoku puzzle game with a clean design and mobile devices in mind.
*   [Swap (‚≠ê159)](https://github.com/nmoroze/swap) - New take on the classic tile-based puzzle game, where you change which character you're controlling to reach your goal.
*   [TransCube (‚≠ê229)](https://github.com/jeroenverfallie/ggo13-transcube) - 2d puzzle platformer based on the concept of transforming into different "blocks", with their unique properties, and making you way to the end of the level with the provided transformations.
*   [Untrusted (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/AlexNisnevich/untrusted) - Meta-JavaScript adventure game by Alex Nisnevich and Greg Shuflin.

### Frameworks/Engines/Libraries / IOS

*   [Babylon.js](https://github.com/BabylonJavaScript/Babylon.js) - Complete JavaScript framework for building 3D games with HTML 5 and WebGL.
*   [CutJavaScript (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/piqnt/cutjs) - Lightweight and fast 2D HTML5 rendering engine for cross-platform game development.

*   [EntityJavaScript (‚≠ê185)](https://github.com/bendangelo/entityjs) - HTML5 JavaScript game engine utlizing the entity-component design.
*   [GameJavaScript (‚≠ê459)](https://github.com/gamejs/gamejs) - GameJs is a JavaScript library for writing 2D games or other interactive graphic applications for the HTML Canvas inspired by PyGame.
*   [Kiwi.js (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/gamelab/kiwi.js) - Blazingly fast mobile & desktop browser based HTML5 game framework. It uses CocoonJavaScript for publishing to the AppStore.
*   [LycheeJavaScript](https://github.com/LazerUnicorns/lycheeJavaScript) - Free HTML5 + native OpenGL Game Engine for Embedded, Console, Mobile, Server and Desktop.
*   [MelonJavaScript](https://github.com/melonjs/melonJavaScript) - HTML5 game framework for 2D games.
*   [PhysicsJavaScript](https://github.com/wellcaffeinated/PhysicsJavaScript) - Modular, extendable, and easy-to-use physics engine for JavaScript.
*   [Superpowers](https://github.com/superpowers) - TypeScript & ThreeJavaScript powered game engine and framework (2D & 3D with WebGL).

## [30. Static Analysis](/content/analysis-tools-dev/static-analysis/week/README.md)

### Programming Languages / [Other](#other-1)

*   [abaplint](https://abaplint.org) ‚Äî Linter for ABAP, written in TypeScript.
*   [gawk --lint](https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html_node/Options.html) ‚Äî Warns about constructs that are dubious or nonportable to other awk implementations.
*   [Astr√©e](https://www.absint.com/astree/index.htm) :copyright: ‚Äî Astr√©e automatically proves the absence of runtime errors and invalid con¬≠current behavior in C/C++ applications. It is sound for floating-point computations, very fast, and exceptionally precise. The analyzer also checks for MISRA/CERT/CWE/Adaptive Autosar coding rules and supports qualification for ISO 26262, DO-178C level A, and other safety standards. Jenkins and Eclipse plugins are available.
*   [.NET Analyzers](https://github.com/DotNetAnalyzers) ‚Äî An organization for the development of analyzers (diagnostics and code fixes) using the .NET Compiler Platform.
*   [clj-kondo (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/borkdude/clj-kondo) ‚Äî A linter for Clojure code that sparks joy. It informs you about potential errors while you are typing.
*   [ameba](https://crystal-ameba.github.io) ‚Äî A static code analysis tool for Crystal.
*   [Dart Code Metrics](https://pub.dev/packages/dart_code_metrics) ‚Äî Additional linter for Dart. Reports code metrics, checks for anti-patterns and provides additional rules for Dart analyzer.
*   [Fix Insight](https://www.tmssoftware.com/site/fixinsight.asp) :copyright: ‚Äî A free IDE Plugin for static code analysis. A *Pro* edition includes a command line tool for automation purposes.
*   [D-scanner (‚≠ê235)](https://github.com/dlang-community/D-Scanner) ‚Äî D-Scanner is a tool for analyzing D source code.
*   [credo (‚≠ê4.6k)](https://github.com/rrrene/credo) ‚Äî A static code analysis tool with a focus on code consistency and teaching.

### Other / [Other](#other-1)

*   [dawnscanner (‚≠ê677)](https://github.com/thesp0nge/dawnscanner) ‚Äî A static analysis security scanner for ruby written web applications. It supports Sinatra, Padrino and Ruby on Rails frameworks.
*   [Angular ESLint (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/angular-eslint/angular-eslint#readme) ‚Äî Linter for Angular projects
*   [kics](https://kics.io/) ‚Äî Find security vulnerabilities, compliance issues, and infrastructure misconfigurations in your infrastructure-as-code. Supports Terraform, Kubernetes, Docker, AWS CloudFormation and Ansible
*   [AzSK](https://azsk.azurewebsites.net/) ‚Äî Secure DevOps kit for Azure (AzSK) provides security IntelliSense, Security Verification Tests (SVTs), CICD scan vulnerabilities, compliance issues, and infrastructure misconfiguration in your infrastructure-as-code. Supports Azure via ARM.
*   [Twiggy](https://rustwasm.github.io/twiggy) ‚Äî Analyzes a binary's call graph to profile code size. The goal is to slim down wasm binary size.
*   [checkmake (‚≠ê865)](https://github.com/mrtazz/checkmake) ‚Äî Linter / Analyzer for Makefiles.
*   [metadata-json-lint (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/voxpupuli/metadata-json-lint) ‚Äî Tool to check the validity of Puppet metadata.json files.
*   [deno\_lint (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/denoland/deno_lint) ‚Äî Official linter for Deno.
*   [oelint-adv (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/priv-kweihmann/oelint-adv) ‚Äî Linter for bitbake recipes used in open-embedded and YOCTO
*   [gherkin-lint (‚≠ê141)](https://github.com/vsiakka/gherkin-lint) ‚Äî A linter for the Gherkin-Syntax written in Javascript.
*   [HTML-Validate](https://html-validate.org/) ‚Äî Offline HTML5 validator.
*   [chart-testing (‚≠ê940)](https://github.com/helm/chart-testing) ‚Äî ct is the the tool for testing Helm charts.  It is meant to be used for linting and testing pull requests.  It automatically detects charts changed against the target branch.
*   [ChkTeX](http://www.nongnu.org/chktex) ‚Äî A linter for LaTex which catches some typographic errors LaTeX oversees.
*   [markdownlint (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/DavidAnson/markdownlint) ‚Äî Node.js -based style checker and lint tool for Markdown/CommonMark files.
*   [Android Lint](http://tools.android.com/tips/lint) ‚Äî Run static analysis on Android projects.
*   [deadnix (‚≠ê211)](https://github.com/astro/deadnix) ‚Äî Scan Nix files for dead code (unused variable bindings)
*   [lintian](https://lintian.debian.org) ‚Äî Static analysis tool for Debian packages.
*   [buf](https://buf.build) ‚Äî Provides a CLI linter that enforces good API design choices and structure
*   [mythril (‚≠ê3k)](https://github.com/ConsenSys/mythril) ‚Äî A symbolic execution framework with batteries included, can be used to find and exploit vulnerabilities in smart contracts automatically.
*   [LibVCS4j (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/uni-bremen-agst/libvcs4j) ‚Äî A Java library that allows existing tools to analyse the evolution of software systems by providing a common API for different version control systems and issue trackers.
*   [ember-template-lint (‚≠ê253)](https://github.com/ember-template-lint/ember-template-lint) ‚Äî Linter for Ember or Handlebars templates.
*   [After the Deadline](https://open.afterthedeadline.com) :warning: ‚Äî Spell, style and grammar checker.
*   [commitlint](https://commitlint.js.org) ‚Äî checks if your commit messages meet the conventional commit format

### More Collections / [Other](#other-1)

*   [Clean code linters](https://github.com/collections/clean-code-linters) ‚Äî A collection of linters in github collections
*   [Code Quality Checker Tools For PHP Projects](https://github.com/collections/code-quality-in-php) ‚Äî A collection of PHP linters in github collections
*   [go-tools (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools) ‚Äî A collection of tools and libraries for working with Go code, including linters and static analysis
